<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="create-an-object">Create an object<a href="#create-an-object" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Create an object" title="Direct link to Create an object" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>This example creates an object in the <code>JeopardyQuestion</code> collection.</p>

<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary><p>Additional information</p></summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>To create an object, specify the following:</p><ul>
<li class="">The object data you want to add</li>
<li class="">The target collection</li>
<li class="">If <a class="" href="/weaviate/concepts/data#multi-tenancy">multi-tenancy</a> is enabled, <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/multi-tenancy">specify the tenant</a></li>
</ul><p>By default, <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#auto-schema">auto-schema</a> creates new collections and adds new properties.</p></div></div></details>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="create-an-object-with-a-specified-vector">Create an object with a specified vector<a href="#create-an-object-with-a-specified-vector" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Create an object with a specified vector" title="Direct link to Create an object with a specified vector" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>When you create an object, you can provide a vector. (For specifying multiple, named vectors, see <a href="#create-an-object-with-named-vectors" class="">below</a>.)</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="create-an-object-with-named-vectors">Create an object with named vectors<a href="#create-an-object-with-named-vectors" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Create an object with named vectors" title="Direct link to Create an object with named vectors" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.24</code></div></div>
<p>When you create an object, you can specify named vectors (if <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/vector-config#define-named-vectors">configured in your collection</a>).</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="create-an-object-with-a-specified-id">Create an object with a specified ID<a href="#create-an-object-with-a-specified-id" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Create an object with a specified ID" title="Direct link to Create an object with a specified ID" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>When you create an object, you can specify an <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/additional-properties#id">ID</a>.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>info</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>If no ID is provided, Weaviate will generate a random <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Universally_unique_identifier" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">UUID</a>.</p></div></div>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="generate-deterministic-ids">Generate deterministic IDs<a href="#generate-deterministic-ids" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Generate deterministic IDs" title="Direct link to Generate deterministic IDs" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>You can generate an ID based on your data object.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>info</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Object IDs are not randomly generated. The same value always generates the same ID.<br>Weaviate throws an error if you provide a duplicate ID. Use deterministic IDs to avoid inserting duplicate objects.</p></div></div>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="go">Go</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. <details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary><p>Additional information</p></summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>To generate deterministic IDs, use one of these methods:</p><ul>
<li class=""><code>generate_uuid5</code> (Python)</li>
<li class=""><code>generateUuid5</code> (TypeScript)</li>
</ul></div></div></details>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="create-an-object-with-cross-references">Create an object with cross-references<a href="#create-an-object-with-cross-references" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Create an object with cross-references" title="Direct link to Create an object with cross-references" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-caution admonition_xJq3 alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>Cross-references and query performance</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Queries involving cross-references can be slower than queries that do not involve cross-references, especially at scale such as for multiple objects or complex queries.</p><p>At the first instance, we strongly encourage you to consider whether you can avoid using cross-references in your data schema. As a scalable AI database, Weaviate is well-placed to perform complex queries with vector, keyword and hybrid searches involving filters. You may benefit from rethinking your data schema to avoid cross-references where possible.</p><p>For example, instead of creating separate &quot;Author&quot; and &quot;Book&quot; collections with cross-references, consider embedding author information directly in Book objects and using searches and filters to find books by author characteristics.</p></div></div>
<!-- -->
<p>You can create an object with cross-references to other objects.</p>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. Check the<!-- --> <a href="/weaviate/release-notes">Release notes</a> <!-- -->for specific versions.<br><br>If a snippet doesn&#x27;t work or you have feedback, please open a<!-- --> <a href="https://github.com/weaviate/docs/issues/new?template=doc_feedback.yml&amp;title=%5BDocumentation+Feedback%5D%3A+&amp;labels=user-feedback&amp;page-url=" target="_blank" rel="noopener class="tabItem_Ymn6"><div><div class="language-py codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-py codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">questions </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> client</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token plain">collections</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token plain">use</span><span class="token <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="create-an-object-with-geocoordinates">Create an object with <code>geoCoordinates</code><a href="#create-an-object-with-geocoordinates" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to create-an-object-with-geocoordinates" title="Direct link to create-an-object-with-geocoordinates" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>Limitations</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Currently, geo-coordinate filtering is limited to the nearest 800 results from the source location, which will be further reduced by any other filter conditions and search parameters.</p><p>If you plan on a densely populated dataset, consider using another strategy such as geo-hashing into a <code>text</code> datatype, and filtering further, such as with a <code>ContainsAny</code> filter.</p></div></div>
<p>If you want to supply a <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/datatypes#geocoordinates"><code>geoCoordinates</code></a> property, you need to specify the <code>latitude</code> and <code>longitude</code> as floating point decimal degrees:</p>
<!-- -->

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="validate-objects-before-creation">Validate objects before creation<a href="#validate-objects-before-creation" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Validate objects before creation" title="Direct link to Validate objects before creation" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Before you create an object, you can <a href="/weaviate/api/rest#tag/objects/post/objects/validate">validate</a> it against the collection definition.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="multiple-vector-embeddings-named-vectors">Multiple vector embeddings (named vectors)<a href="#multiple-vector-embeddings-named-vectors" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Multiple vector embeddings (named vectors)" title="Direct link to Multiple vector embeddings (named vectors)" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in v1.24.0</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Weaviate collections support multiple named vectors.</p></div></div>
<p>Collections can have multiple <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#named-vectors">named vectors</a>.</p>
<p>The vectors in a collection can have their own configurations. Each vector space can set its own index, its own compression algorithm, and its own vectorizer. This means you can use different vectorization models, and apply different distance metrics, to the same object.</p>
<p>To work with named vectors, adjust your queries to specify a target vector for <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/similarity#named-vectors">vector search</a> or <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/hybrid#named-vectors">hybrid search</a> queries.</p>
